- Productos vendidos ahora muestra nombre del producto con desglose cajas/unidades.
- Alpine.js agregado al layout para tabs interactivos.
- Reportes: filtro de pestañas "Ventas por Evento" / "Ventas Directas" con listado completo de ventas directas y totales por método.

## Key Decisions
- Guard `staff` separado del guard `web` para autenticación con username/password.
- Contraseñas almacenadas con cast `hashed`.
- `Config` model (tabla clave-valor) para QR, tipos de evento, settings de contrato y marca de agua.
- Marca de agua usa disco `public` para doble acceso (URL y disco local).
- Venta directa agrupada por día con `event_id` = `Venta Directa - YYYY-MM-DD`.
- Reportes con rutas separadas (`/reports` y `/reports/logs`) y tabs con Alpine.js en vez de JS manual.
- Botón de confirmación siempre habilitado, validación移ida a `submitSale()`.
- Distribución de productos con gráfico de torta CSS (`conic-gradient`) sin librerías externas.

- Probar flujo completo de venta directa con los nuevos cambios.

## Critical Context
- `watermark_image` se almacena en `storage/app/public/watermarks/` (disco `public`).
- `EventController::downloadContract` resuelve watermark con `storage_path('app/public/...')`.
- `Settings::updateContractSettings` usa `store('watermarks', 'public')`.
- `event_id` de venta directa = `Venta Directa - YYYY-MM-DD`, detectado con `str_starts_with($validated['event_id'], 'Venta Directa')`.
- `SaleController::processSale`: `client_name` es `nullable`, default `'Venta Directa'`.
- Bug de stack overflow en `sales/direct` corregido: `updateTotals()` y `updateChange()` ahora son independientes sin llamadas circulares.
- Reportes Página 2 movida a `/reports/logs`, los tabs de Página 1/Página 2 usan `<a>` links.
- Alpine.js agregado para tabs "Ventas por Evento" / "Ventas Directas" en reportes.
- Último evento cerrado: 6 tarjetas con datos (evento, facturas, venta más alta con cliente, total, métodos, productos + torta).

**Input:**

**Output:**
```
<?php

namespace App\Http\Controllers;

use App\Models\Event;
use App\Models\Sale;
use Illuminate\Http\Request;

class ReportController extends Controller
{
    public function index()
    {
        $events = Event::orderBy('date', 'desc')->get();
        $closedEvents = $events->where('status', 'Cerrado');
        
        $totalSales = 0;
        foreach ($closedEvents as $event) {
            $sales = Sale::where('event_id', $event->id)->get();
            $totalSales += $sales->sum('amount');
        }

        return view('reports.index', compact('events', 'closedEvents', 'totalSales'));
    }

    public function show(Event $event)
    {
        $sales = Sale::where('event_id', $event->id)->orderBy('id', 'desc')->get();
        $totalAmount = $sales->sum('amount');
        
        return view('reports.show', compact('event', 'sales', 'totalAmount'));
    }

    public function destroy(Event $event)
    {
        $event->delete();
        return redirect()->route('reports.index')->with('success', 'Evento eliminado.');
    }

    public function getEventTotal(string $eventId): float
    {
        return Sale::where('event_id', $eventId)->sum('amount');
    }

    public function downloadPdf(Event $event)
    {
        $sales = Sale::where('event_id', $event->id)->orderBy('id', 'desc')->get();
        $totalAmount = $sales->sum('amount');
        
        $html = view('pdf.report', compact('event', 'sales', 'totalAmount'))->render();
        
        $pdf = \Barryvdh\DomPDF\Facade\Pdf::loadHTML($html);
        return $pdf->download("Reporte_{$event->client_name}.pdf");
    }
}
```

```
23:     }

26:     {

28:         $totalAmount = $sales->sum('amount');
29:         
30:         return view('reports.show', compact('event', 'sales', 'totalAmount'));
31:     }

34:     {
35:         $event->delete();

37:     }
38: 
39:     public function getEventTotal(string $eventId): float
40:     {
41:         return Sale::where('event_id', $eventId)->sum('amount');
```

```
214:                         <span class="text-[0.65rem] font-bold text-blue-600 uppercase">Cambio sugerido</span>
215:                         <span class="text-xl font-bold text-blue-700" id="change-display">0 Bs</span>
216:                     </div>
217:                 </div>
218: 
219:                 <button type="button" onclick="submitSale()" class="w-full bg-slate-900 text-white py-3.5 rounded-xl font-bold hover:bg-black transition-all shadow-lg active:scale-[0.98]" id="submit-btn" disabled>
220:                     Confirmar Operación
221:                 </button>
222:             </div>
223:         </div>
224:     </div>
225: </div>
226: 
227: <script>
228: let cart = [];
229: let selectedItem = '';
230: let selectedType = 'Caja';
231: 
232: function openModal(id) { document.getElementById(id).classList.remove('hidden'); }
233: function closeModal(id) { document.getElementById(id).classList.add('hidden'); }
234: 
235: function setPaymentMethod(method) {
236:     document.getElementById('payment_method').value = method;
237:     document.querySelectorAll('.payment-btn').forEach(btn => {
238:         if (btn.dataset.method === method) {
239:             btn.className = 'payment-btn flex-1 py-2 rounded-lg text-[0.7rem] font-bold border transition-all bg-slate-800 text-white border-slate-800 shadow-sm';
240:         } else {
241:             btn.className = 'payment-btn flex-1 py-2 rounded-lg text-[0.7rem] font-bold border transition-all bg-white text-text-muted border-border-subtle hover:bg-slate-50';
242:         }
243:     });
244:     const cashSection = document.getElementById('cash-section');
245:     if (method === 'Efectivo') {
246:         cashSection.className = 'flex flex-col gap-1 p-3 rounded-xl transition-colors bg-emerald-50 border border-emerald-100';
247:     } else {
248:         cashSection.className = 'flex flex-col gap-1 p-3 rounded-xl transition-colors bg-slate-50 border border-border-subtle';
249:     }
250: }
251: 
252: function showItemOptions() {
253:     const select = document.getElementById('select-item');
254:     selectedItem = select.value;
255:     const option = select.options[select.selectedIndex];
256:     const imgDisplay = document.getElementById('direct-product-image');
257:     const img = document.getElementById('direct-selected-img');
258:     const name = document.getElementById('direct-product-name');
259:     
260:     if (selectedItem) {
261:         document.getElementById('item-options').classList.remove('hidden');
262:         
263:         const imageBox = option.dataset.imageBox;
264:         const imageUnit = option.dataset.imageUnit;
265:         
266:         if (imageBox || imageUnit) {
267:             const imageUrl = imageBox ? '/storage/' + imageBox : '/storage/' + imageUnit;
268:             img.src = imageUrl;
269:             img.style.display = 'block';
270:             name.textContent = selectedItem;
271:             imgDisplay.classList.remove('hidden');
272:             imgDisplay.classList.add('flex');
273:         } else {
274:             imgDisplay.classList.add('hidden');
275:             imgDisplay.classList.remove('flex');
276:         }
277:     } else {
278:         document.getElementById('item-options').classList.add('hidden');
279:         imgDisplay.classList.add('hidden');
280:         imgDisplay.classList.remove('flex');
281:     }
282: }
283: 
284: function setItemType(type) {
285:     selectedType = type;
286:     document.querySelectorAll('.type-btn').forEach(btn => {
287:         if (btn.dataset.type === type) {
288:             btn.className = 'type-btn flex-1 py-1.5 rounded-md text-xs font-bold transition-all bg-brand-accent text-white shadow-sm';
289:         } else {
290:             btn.className = 'type-btn flex-1 py-1.5 rounded-md text-xs font-bold transition-all bg-white text-text-muted border border-border-subtle';
291:         }
292:     });
293: }
294: 
295: function addToCart() {
296:     if (!selectedItem) return;
297:     const qty = parseInt(document.getElementById('item-qty').value) || 1;
298:     const inventory = @json($inventory);
299:     const item = inventory.find(i => i.name === selectedItem);
300:     const price = selectedType === 'Caja' ? item.price_per_box : item.price_per_unit;
301:     const subtotal = price * qty;
302:     
303:     cart.push({ name: selectedItem, quantity: qty, type: selectedType, subtotal });
304:     renderCart();
305:     
306:     document.getElementById('select-item').value = '';
307:     document.getElementById('item-options').classList.add('hidden');
308:     document.getElementById('item-qty').value = 1;
309: }
310: 
311: function renderCart() {
312:     const container = document.getElementById('cart-items');
313:     const emptyCart = document.getElementById('empty-cart');
314:     
315:     if (cart.length === 0) {
316:         emptyCart.classList.remove('hidden');
317:         container.innerHTML = '';
318:         container.appendChild(emptyCart);
319:     } else {
320:         emptyCart.classList.add('hidden');
321:         let html = '';
322:         cart.forEach((it, idx) => {
323:             html += `
324:                 <div class="bg-white p-3 rounded-lg border border-border-subtle flex justify-between items-center shadow-sm">
325:                     <div>
326:                         <p class="text-[0.8rem] font-bold text-text-main leading-none">${it.name}</p>
327:                         <p class="text-[0.65rem] text-text-muted font-medium">${it.quantity} ${it.type}(s)</p>
328:                     </div>
329:                     <div class="flex items-center gap-3">
330:                         <span class="text-[0.8rem] font-bold text-brand-accent">${it.subtotal.toLocaleString()} Bs</span>
331:                         <button onclick="removeFromCart(${idx})" class="text-red-300 hover:text-red-500 transition-colors">
332:                             <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M18 6 6 18"/><path d="m6 6 12 12"/></svg>
333:                         </button>
334:                     </div>
335:                 </div>
336:             `;
337:         });
338:         container.innerHTML = html;
339:     }
340:     updateTotal();
341: }
342: 
343: function removeFromCart(idx) {
344:     cart.splice(idx, 1);
345:     renderCart();
346: }
347: 
348: function updateTotal() {
349:     const total = cart.reduce((acc, curr) => acc + curr.subtotal, 0);
350:     document.getElementById('total-display').textContent = total.toLocaleString() + ' Bs';
351:     
352:     const method = document.getElementById('payment_method').value;
353:     if (method !== 'Efectivo') {
354:         document.getElementById('cash_received').value = total;
355:     }
356:     
357:     updateChange();
358:     
359:     const submitBtn = document.getElementById('submit-btn');
360:     const cash = parseFloat(document.getElementById('cash_received').value) || 0;
361:     submitBtn.disabled = cart.length === 0 || (method === 'Efectivo' && cash < total);
362: }
363: 
364: function updateChange() {
365:     const total = cart.reduce((acc, curr) => acc + curr.subtotal, 0);
366:     const cash = parseFloat(document.getElementById('cash_received').value) || 0;
367:     const change = cash > total ? cash - total : 0;
368:     document.getElementById('change-display').textContent = change.toLocaleString() + ' Bs';
369:     updateTotal();
370: }
371: 
372: function submitSale() {
373:     if (cart.length === 0) return;
374:     
375:     const method = document.getElementById('payment_method').value;
376:     const cash = method === 'Efectivo' ? parseFloat(document.getElementById('cash_received').value) : 0;
377:     
378:     let form = document.getElementById('sale-form');
379:     let itemsInput = document.createElement('input');
380:     itemsInput.type = 'hidden';
381:     itemsInput.name = 'items';
382:     itemsInput.value = JSON.stringify(cart);
383:     form.appendChild(itemsInput);
384:     
385:     if (method === 'Efectivo') {
386:         let cashInput = document.createElement('input');
387:         cashInput.type = 'hidden';
388:         cashInput.name = 'cash_received';
389:         cashInput.value = cash;
390:         form.appendChild(cashInput);
391:     }
392:     
393:     form.submit();
394: }
395: </script>
396: @endsection

(End of file - total 396 lines)
</content>
```

```
296: function addToCart() {
297:     const select = document.getElementById('product-select');
298:     const qty = parseInt(document.getElementById('sale-qty').value) || 1;
299:     const option = select.options[select.selectedIndex];
300:     
301:     if (!option.value) return;
302:     
303:     const priceBox = parseFloat(option.dataset.priceBox);
304:     const priceUnit = parseFloat(option.dataset.priceUnit);
305:     const price = currentType === 'Caja' ? priceBox : priceUnit;
306:     const subtotal = price * qty;
307:     
308:     cart.push({ name: option.value, quantity: qty, type: currentType, subtotal: subtotal });
309:     updateCart();
310: }
311: 
312: function updateCart() {
313:     const container = document.getElementById('cart-items');
314:     container.innerHTML = cart.map((item, idx) => `
315:         <div class="bg-white p-3 rounded-lg border border-border-subtle flex justify-between items-center shadow-sm">
316:             <div>
317:                 <p class="text-[0.8rem] font-bold text-text-main leading-none">${item.name}</p>
318:                 <p class="text-[0.65rem] text-text-muted font-medium">${item.quantity} ${item.type}(s)</p>
319:             </div>
320:             <div class="flex items-center gap-3">
321:                 <span class="text-[0.8rem] font-bold text-brand-accent">${item.subtotal.toLocaleString()} Bs</span>
322:                 <button type="button" onclick="removeFromCart(${idx})" class="text-red-300 hover:text-red-500"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M18 6 6 18"/><path d="m6 6 12 12"/></svg></button>
323:             </div>
324:         </div>
325:     `).join('');
326:     
327:     const total = cart.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.subtotal, 0);
328:     document.getElementById('total-display').textContent = total.toLocaleString() + ' Bs';
329:     
330:     const cash = parseFloat(document.getElementById('cash-received').value) || 0;
331:     document.getElementById('change-display').textContent = (cash > total ? cash - total : 0).toLocaleString() + ' Bs';
332: }
333: 
334: document.getElementById('cash-received').addEventListener('input', updateCart);
335: 
336: function removeFromCart(idx) {
337:     cart.splice(idx, 1);
338:     updateCart();
339: }
340:
```

```
281: <script>
282: function openModal(id) { document.getElementById(id).classList.remove('hidden'); }
283: function closeModal(id) { document.getElementById(id).classList.add('hidden'); }
284: 
285: function updateAuditFields() {
286:     const select = document.querySelector('select[name="inventory_id"]');
287:     const option = select.options[select.selectedIndex];
288:     if (option.value) {
289:         document.getElementById('audit_boxes').value = option.dataset.boxes || 0;
290:         document.getElementById('audit_loose').value = option.dataset.loose || 0;
291:     } else {
292:         document.getElementById('audit_boxes').value = 0;
293:         document.getElementById('audit_loose').value = 0;
294:     }
295: }
```
